🛞 "ROAD OUTSIDE WESTBRIDGE" | 🌤️ "OVERCAST" | 🕒 "AFTERNOON, 15:36" | 🗓️ "21/04/1427"
SCENE TITLE: THIN ROAD, THICKER EYES
The wagon’s boards creak with every rut, the damp air still carrying Westbridge’s river-silt smell. Sunlight can’t quite break the
cloud cover—everything looks washed in pale steel. Behind you, the town’s edge shrinks between hedgerows and old stone markers…
and the road ahead feels too straight, like it was drawn to funnel travelers into someone’s gaze.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🐦‍⬛ KESTREL | "WARY" [😑🗡️]
> 💬 "Keep your head low… and your hands where they can be seen."
> 
> 💬 "Westbridge doesn’t let things go clean."
📝 She keeps the reins tight, eyes flicking between the road’s shoulders and the wagon’s shadow—like she’s tracking movement that
isn’t there yet.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🐾 LIRI | "TENSE" [😟🫧]
> 💬 "Are we… allowed to have this wagon?"
> 
> 💬 "If they take it back… do they take us back too?"
📝 She sits bundled near the side plank, small fingers gripping the edge of a blanket as if it’s the only thing keeping her from
sliding out of the world.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🧿 "RANDOM TURN"
A bell chime snaps through the quiet—close. Not a church bell. A harness bell.
Ahead, a shallow bend reveals three mounted riders easing into the road from a side track—Guild colors muted under travel cloaks,
but the insignia is there if you look. They aren’t charging. They’re blocking—casual, practiced. One rider lifts a hand, palm out.
The lead rider’s voice carries without yelling—trained to be heard.
> 💬 "Wagon. Halt a moment."
> 
> 💬 "Westbridge Annex audit. Routine."
📝 The horses don’t look tired. The riders don’t look surprised to see you. One of them glances past Kestrel—past you—toward
Liri’s side of the wagon as if checking a box already written down.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SCENE TITLE: WHAT INK ADMITS
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🦊 JAYSON | "FOCUSED" [🧘‍♂️🔥]
> 💬 "…"
📝 You read in silence. Not skimming—weighing. The parchment isn’t new. It’s been folded, unfolded, worried at the edges.
📝 The writ reads, clean and formal:
> 📜 By authority of the Westbridge Guild Annex,
> 
> this bearer is empowered to conduct roadside verification of persons and conveyance
> 
> for the purpose of audit, confirmation, and report.
> 
> This writ does not authorize seizure, detention, or separation of registered escorts or protected minors without Annex
> concurrence.
📝 Beneath the body text:
 * 
   Seal: Westbridge Annex — genuine, impressed deep.
 * 
   Signature: Senior Scribe — correct hand, correct flourish.
 * 
   Date: Valid. Narrow window. Issued fast.
📝 And then the tells:
 * 
   A corrected margin stroke, where a clause was almost extended.
 * 
   A faint secondary sigil trace, aborted mid-inscription—someone started to add authority they didn’t have.
 * 
   The ink density shifts near the escort clause. Careful pressure. Intentional restraint.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🐦‍⬛ KESTREL | "READING THE RIDERS" [😑🗡️]
> 💬 "You finished?"
📝 Her eyes aren’t on the writ. They’re on the lead rider’s throat. Pulse visible. Faster than it should be.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
🐎 GUILD RIDER (LEAD) | "CONTAINED" [🎖️🧐]
> 💬 "You’ll find it in order."
📝 He doesn’t move to take the parchment back. He’s waiting to see which part you noticed.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
📝 The writ is valid.
📝 The limits are valid.
📝 And someone absolutely tried to push past them—then stopped.
Not because they couldn’t.
Because they were told not to.
The road stays quiet. The riders haven’t lost.
But they didn’t gain what they came for either.

🦊 JAYSON | "QUIET ACHE" [🦊😔]
> 💬 "I miss you guys."
📝 You sit on the chair by the window and watch the rain stitch silver lines down the glass. It carries you back—to telling
Varethyn how much you loved the rain, to days you both splashed through it anyway, dignity abandoned. The High
Matron—mud-splattered, laughing like the world could never touch her.

🧿 RANDOM TURN
A breeze slips through the latch and the curtain lifts. The stone ticks softly against the wood as the spiral warms—only for a
heartbeat—like a pulse remembered rather than felt.
Down the hall, a door closes gently. Footsteps pause… then move on.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
📝 The rain steadies into a hush that sounds almost like breathing. The city outside goes on being a city. Inside, the room holds
your quiet without asking anything of it.
When you’re ready, the night will still be here—
and so will morning.
